vastut: Buddha ka marg dhnyan margi hai, sankalp margi hai, bhaktimargi nahin hai. purush (purush chitt) v stri (strain chitt ) ke chetna ke kendra bhi bhinn hai . Purush mulat: man (Mind) kendrit hai . uska sara jor baudghik hai . wah har chij ko tark vitark ke aadhar par hi tolta hai . Tark karne men bhav ki gunjaish nahin rah pati . Tarkvaan vyakti hi sankalp aasani se kar pata hai . Isliye tarkvaan vyakti kathor bhi hota hai . Yhi vyakti (purush-chitt) buddh ke marg ke anukul hai . Purushon men bahut kam log hi strain-chitt wale milengen . Aur striyon men bahut kam log hi purush chitr wale milengen . Dusri taraf stri (strain-chitt) ki chetna ka tal bhavna pradhan hai . Prem ki matra, bhav ki matra stri men pragadh hoti hai . Samrapan usmen sahaj hota hai . hosh ko khone men, swayn ke prati besudh hone men use aasani lagti hai . Yahi stri ke aayam Buddh ke marg ke pratikul padate hain . Buddh ka marg to hosh (samma-sati) v sankalp (adhishthan) ka marg hai .
